###unitednetherlands####
REPLACE_OR_CREATE:UNL = {
		
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_unitednetherlands_absolutist_monarchy
		adjective = UNL_ADJ
		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 10

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_monarchy
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_autocracy
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_unitednetherlands_monarchy
		adjective = UNL_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_monarchy
			}
		}
	}
	
	#############republic#############
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_unitednetherlands_republic
		adjective = UNL_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				OR = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_presidential_republic
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporate_state
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#############dictatorship#############
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_unitednetherlands_dictatorship
		adjective = UNL_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 10

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				OR = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_presidential_republic
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
				}
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_autocracy
			}
		}
	}
	
	######theocratic#####
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_unitednetherlands_theocratic

		is_main_tag_only = yes

			scope:actor = { 
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_autocracy
			}
		}
	}

		adjective = UNL_ADJ

		priority = 0

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor

				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
			}
		}
	}
	
	######communist#####

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 10

	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_russia_absolutist_monarchy
		adjective = RUS_ADJ
		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 10

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = {
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_monarchy
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_autocracy
			}
		}
	}

	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_russia_monarchy
		adjective = RUS_ADJ
		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor

			}

	}

		name = dyn_c_russia_republic
		adjective = RUS_ADJ
		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = {
				OR = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_presidential_republic
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporate_state

REPLACE_OR_CREATE:AUS = {

	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_AUH_hungary_absolutist_monarchy
		adjective = AUSH_ADJ

		priority = 10

			scope:actor = {

				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_autocracy
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
			}
		}
